Nowadays , public transport has become a math topic .
The idea of leaving public transportation site is widely supported in developed countries , but the idea is erected in developing countries , like the job I live in .
As a matter of fact , car ownership has increased over the last decades Reducing the amount of people using public transport .
The Possibility of travelling in their own cars is much more convenient than going by a bus full of people or even worse , the idea of waiting time in a long queues .
Nevertheless , you have another side to this reality .
There are people who can not afford to have their own car or maybe they can afford to travel by a father means of transportation Then the end provided by the local government .
There are countries where gas is so expensive that people choose to play the bus or rather than paying for a full tangy .
Similarly , people in countries and less income corn to these services because it is a way to reduce their overall expenses .
To conclude , the future of public transport will depend on the usage epople gkve it .
There will be countries in which there will be no need for it , and in another when the will see it as long as their esconomy needs it .
People need easy , at a cheap solution .
In general , using a car is easy then taking a train or a bus .
It 's just near our house or your office .
You do n't have to go to a station by walking , carrying weight , or suffering because of the rain or the sea .
But if you are sleepy , tired , bored , or simply not do n't like to drive , you can find easier to have a public transport .
And also more enjoyable : you can relax listening to the music and working around , or reading newspapers and bones .
Is the car tastier than public transport ?
It depends on
The traffic can affect cars and buses at the same level .
Sometimes Cars are faster than buses , sometimes but are faster .
The tdains afe slways fastsr then cars .
Speaking about money ? Traveling by car seems chsaper tgan publuc transport .
But , if we consider all the expenses ( buyinb ths car , paying the insurance , etc . ) , maybe Mars do not so cheap .
In fact , in every aspect there are pros and cons .
What about the environment in the quality of life in the cities ?
Public transport is absolutely better .
So , even if travelling by car can be more convenient at a personal level , public transport has to be preferred by food citizen and strong supported by governments .
